 unhone jameen ke vaaste paise jutaney ke liye mujhe apane saare gahane de die
 ' aakhirkaar, farvari 2017 ko aspataal shuru hone par saidul kaa sapana saakaar hua
 Saidul inaugurated the hospital at the hands of his new sister Srishti
 kareeb 11 kilometre ke daayre main sabase najdiki aspataal hone se sthaneey nivaasiyon se kaaphi acchhee pratikriya mil rahi he
 On the way to the hospital, e-rickshaw driver Sojol Das said, 'now there is discussion everywhere and people talk about the hospital in the area
 ' Now work is going on to make this hospital equipped with 50 beds, X-rays and ECG facilities
 saidul ne kaha, 'vartmaan main yah domanjila bhawan he lekin hamaari yojana ise chaar manjila banane kii he
 On the opening day of the hospital, our doctors treated 286 patients here
 samay or sansaadhan kii kami ke chalate anek logon ko ve nahin dekh paae
 i am sure that when the hospital is fully operational, it will benefit the people of about 100 villages
 ' Many people have been influenced by Saidul's big dreams and passion for realizing it
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne apane 'man kii baat' kaarykram main saidul ke prayaason kii saraahna kii
 The 40-year-old taxi driver said that he was quite excited when PM Modi discussed the hospital
 unhone kaha, 'piem modi ke zikr karne ke baad se kai logon ne mujhase sampark kiya he
 Some local contractors have helped me by providing sand, brick and cement to complete the building work
 chennai ke ek doctor ne mere aspataal main apni seva dene or marijon kaa ilaaj karne kii ichha jataai he
 ' unhone bataaya ki vartmaan main aath doctor aspataal se jude hai, jo yahaan abhi muft main apni seva de rahe hai
 Saidul, however, said that his plan is to provide healthcare at the bare minimum fee necessary for the maintenance of the hospital
 haddirog vibhaag ke prabharee dow
 Dheresh Chaudhary greatly appreciated Saidul's efforts
 unhone kaha, 'aspataal bananaa bada kaam he
 This is unimaginable for a low-income Saidul
 ham sabhi unke saath hai
 ' doctor kaa enjio 'benchori' aspataal ko chikitsa upkaran muhaiyaa karwaata he
 The comments saidul ne kaha, 'ab hamaare saath kai log hai
 i feel that to fulfill my dream, i can now also think ahead
 shaayad, main sirf ek aspataal banaakar nahin rukuunga or nae sapane kii talash main jaaoongaa
 'video: Jharkhand girls' exploits in Spain saidul taxi chalaate samay apni gaadi main baithe paisanger ko apane kagajaat or logon se mili daan kii parchiyaan dikhaata magar zyaadaatar log unki koi madad karne se inkaar kar dete the
 However some people also helped him
 inhen logon main kolkata kii yuvati sristi ghosh bhi hai jo unki dukh bhari kahani sunakar dukhi ho gayi or unhone aspataal ke liye apane puure maheene kaa vetan dene kaa faisla liya
 Saidul said, 'I have found my lost sister in the form of Srishti
 meri kahani sunne ke baad sristi or unki maa ne meraa phone number liya or mujhe baad main phone kiya
 i had no faith that she would call me
 magar, jab vah apana pehla vetan lekar mere paas ai to main emosnal ho gaya
 ' aparichiton ke saath-saath saidul kii patni shamima ne bhi unka hausala badhaayaa
 He said, 'if i do not get the support of my wife, nothing is possible
 jab maine aspataal banane kii thaanee to mere najdiki logon ne mujhe pagal samajhakar mujhase duriyaan bana leen magar meri patni hameshaa mere saath khadi raheen
 He gave me all his jewelry to raise money for the land
 ' Ultimately, Saidul's dream came true when the hospital started in February 2017
 saidul ne apni nai bahan sristi ke haathon aspataal kaa udghaatan karavaaya
 Being the nearest hospital within a radius of about 11 km, there is a good response from the local residents
 aspataal jate samay i-rickshaw chaalak sozol das ne bataaya, 'har taraf ab charchaa hoti he or ilaake main aspataal ke bare main log baaten karte hai
 ' ab is aspataal ko 50 bed, eks-re or isiji kii suvidha se las banane kii disha main kaam chal rahaa he
 Saidul said, 'currently it is a two-storey building but we plan to make it four storeyed
 aspataal ke udghaatan ke din hamaare doctoron ne yahaan 286 marijon kaa ilaaj kiya
 Due to lack of time and resources, they could not see many people
 mujhe pakkaa bharosa he ki jab aspataal puri tarah se chaalu ho jayega to isse kareeb 100 gaanvon ke logon ko phayda hoga
 ' saidul ke bade sapane dekhne or use saakaar karne ke junun se kaaphi log prabhavit hue hai
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi praised Saidul's efforts in his 'mann Ki Baat' program
 40 varshiya taxi driver ne kaha ki piem modi ne jab aspataal kii charchaa kii to vah kaaphi utsahit hue
 He said, 'since mentioning PM Modi many people have contacted me
 kuch sthaneey thekedaaron ne imaarat ke kaam ko puraa karne ke liye ret, eent or cement muhaiyaa karwaakar meri madad kii he
 a doctor from Chennai has expressed my desire to serve in my hospital and treat patients
 ' He said that at present eight doctors are associated with the hospital, who are giving their services here for free
 haalanki saidul ne kaha ki unki yojana he ki aspataal ke rakrakhaav ke liye jaruri maatr nunatam shulk par swasthya seva muhaiyaa karaane kii he
 Dr
 in charge of Orthopedics Department
 dhiresh choudhary ne saidul ke prayaason kii kaaphi saraahna kii
 He said, 'it is a big job to build a hospital
 atyant kam aamadani vaale saidul ke liye yah kaam acolpaneey he
 We are all with them

 siries ke tahat ab tak hue teenon maichon main ajinkya buree tarah naakaam rahe hai or unke khate main 13, 1 (rajkot), 23, 26 (vikhakhapattanam) or 0 (mohali) ke score hi darj hai
 The comments ye vahiin rahane hai jinhone newjiland ke khilaaf siries main rahane ne teen maichon kii chah pariyon main ek baar naabad rahete hue 69
 He scored 347 runs at an average of 40 with 188 being his highest score
 westeindies ke khilaaf isi varsh hui siries main bhi rahane ne ek shatak sahit 243 ran banaae the
 In such a situation, the cricket lovers are busy in the uproar that what has happened against England which Rahane has not been able to score even a half-century
 vishakhpattanam test kii donon pariyon main to rahane ne wicket par nazren jamaane ke baad apana wicket ganvaaya
 In the Mohali test, he had to bear the brunt of not being able to read Adil Rashid's googly
 cricket jaankaron kii raay maane to ajinkya kii takanic main kuch bhi galat nahin he or ek acha score karne ke baad unke balle se phir ran nikalne lagenge
 Certainly, the re-runs of Team India from Ajinkya's bat will be good news for Team India and cricket lovers

 aagaamee loksabhaa chunaav main bhaajapa ko chunauti dene ke liye vipakshi ekajutata ko lekar chal rahe prayaason ke bich congress ne aaj kaha ki vahi (congress) vipakshi dalon kii ‘ekta kii dhuree’ banegi or keval rahul gandhi hi pradhanmantri narendra modi kaa vikalp honge
 Randeep Surjewala, the head and chief spokesperson of the Congress's media department claimed in the interview, 'modiji's option is the only and only Rahulji
 koi or nahin ho saktaa
 The Congress and the people of the country want to see Rahulji as the next Prime Minister of the country
 ’rahul gandhi ne rock concert main pahani 63 hajaar kii jacket, congress boli - 'ye to 700 rupee main milti he' Surjewala said this in response to the question that in the next election, who will be the choice of Prime Minister Modi? He said, 'today there are two models
 
 
 modi model (jisamen vah) din main chah baar kapade badalte hai, apane kapadon kii krij bhi kharaab nahin hone dete, apni veshbhusha par jitna samay lagaate hai shaayad shashan par utana samay nahin lagaate
 The second model is that of Rahul Gandhi, which is based on simplicity, simplicity and cleanliness
 rahul gandhi raajnneeti main apni bebaaki, paardarshita or eemaandaaree ke liye mashhoor hue hai
 He is never afraid to take harsh decisions
 ’ Asked about opposition unity, he said that BJD, Shiv Sena and now TDP are gradually separating from NDA while 'congress is becoming the axis of unity of different parties
 ‘yah ekta 2019 main badlaav kaa aadhaar banegi
 It is known that the Shiv Sena has already made it clear that it will not contest the 2019 elections with the BJP
 centre main sattarudh rajg ke anya bade ghatak tedepa ne bhi pichley dinon pesh kiye gaye aam bajet par niraashaa jataayi he
 When asked about the allegations of disappointment of the middle class in the Union Budget presented in Parliament by Union Finance Minister Arun Jaitley, Surjewala said that the Modi government has only cheated the middle class and the employed people with jumals, nothing
 notebandi or jiesti kii sabase badi maar bhi isi varg par sabase adhik padi
 He said that according to the Finance Minister, this category also gives the highest tax
 unhen yah lagata he ki sabase zyada amir yahi varg he jabaki sachai yah he ki sabase zyada mehanatakash or eemaandaar yahi varg he
 Today, this class is paying a great price for inflation
 isiilie madhyam varg is baat ko acchhee tarah samaj gaya he ki modi sarkaar main ‘baaten bahut or kaam kuch bhi nahin
 ' varsh 2018-19 kaa aam bajet pesh karte hue vitt mantri ne kar chukaane ke maamle main naukareepesha varg kii prashansa karne ke baavjood unhen iskar ke maamle main koi badi raahat nahin di he
 Asked about the strategy of the Congress in the assembly elections to be held in eight states including Karnataka this year, Surjewala said, "we are confident that the Congress will come back to power in Karnataka, the most important state for growth
" hamane jis tarah se karnataka main vikaas kaa ek model pesh kiya he, chaahe vah eve bill ho yaa karnataka sarkaar kii anya yojanaayen hon, ab bharat sarkaar bhi maanati he ki unka puure desh main kriyanvayan hona chahie
 ' unhone kaha ki agle charan main madhya pradesh, chhattisgarh, rajasthan aadi main jo chunaav honge, unka trailor do din pehle rajasthan ke up-chunaav main aa chukaa jahaan congress ne do loksabhaa evam ek vidhansabha seat jiti
 He said, 'this anger is not against the Vasundhara Raje government alone
 yah modi sarkaar evam raaje sarkaar ke jumalon se thagi gai janata dwaara congress ko waapas laane kii bayaar he
 In the by-election results announced last week, the Congress shocked the ruling BJP by winning the Ajmer and Alwar Lok Sabha and Mandalgarh assembly seats as the saffron party held all three seats
 varsh 2018 main karnataka, meghalaya, tripura, nagaland, madhya pradesh, chhattisgarh, rajasthan or mizoram main vidhansabha ke chunaav hone hai
 When asked three priorities of Rahul Gandhi as party president, Surjewala said that his first priority is restructuring and change of the organization of the All India Congress and its units across the country
 unki anya praathamikta ek aise ‘vijan’ ko taiyaar kar lagu karnaa he jisase kisaanon ko unki upaj kaa uchit laabh mil sake
 In this vision, there will be measures to create jobs in private and government sectors
 unhone kaha, ‘modiji ke model main 12 udyogpatiyon kii madad he jabaki rahul gandhi ke model main madhyam evam laghu udyog kshetra ko praathamikta dekar unke liye maukey, bazaar or rin uplabdh karana hoga
 He said that the third priority is social peace and restoration of brotherhood
 ‘modiji yah bhul gayi hai ki jab saamaajik tanabana tuutata he to vikaas kaa pahiyaa tham jaataa he
 Asked when the party's first plenary would take place after Rahul became Congress president, he said that its date has not been decided yet
 kintu varsh 2019 or uske baad ke samay main is desh kii sanrachana ke liye ek nayi drushti congress is adhiveshan ke madhyam se desh ko degi
 The comments VIDEO : ganatantr diwas parade ke dauraan chhathi pankti main rahul gandhi, congress ne jataayaa aitraaj Asked about the apprehension of the secularism of the Congress in the minds of the minority sections due to the perception of Congress following the path of 'soft Hindutva' after the Gujarat elections, he said, 'religion is a matter of personal faith
 rahulji shivbhakt hai
 If he goes for worship and personal belief, then why should any person or political party have any objection? He said that this country belongs to all Hindus, Muslims, Sikhs, Christians, Jains, Buddhists etc
 isamen congress kaa atoot vishwaas he kyonki yah bhaavana samvidhan or desh kii aatma main bhi he
 Congress and the soul of the country are one
 unhone kaha, ‘ham is paripati ko aaajeevan nibhaaenge
 Rahul Gandhi is also committed to this
 ’ Input: Bhasharahul Gandhi wore a jacket of 63 thousand at the rock concert, Congress said - 'this is available for Rs 700' surajevaala ne yah baat is sawaal ke jawaab main kahi ki agle chunaav main pradhanmantri modi kaa vikalp koun banegaa? unhone kaha, ‘aaj do model hai
 
 
 The Modi model (in which he) changes clothes six times a day, does not let the crease of his clothes deteriorate, spending as much time on his costumes, perhaps not spending as much time on governance
 doosraa model he rahul gandhi kaa, jo saadagi, saralata or safagoi par aadhaarit he
 Rahul Gandhi has been known for his frankness, transparency and honesty in politics
 vah kathor nirnay lene se bhi kabhi nahin darate
 ' vipakshi ekta ke bare main poochne par unhone kaha ki bijd, shivasena or ab tedepa dhire-dhire rajg se alag ho rahe hai jabaki ‘congress vibhinn dalon kii ekta kii dhuree banati ja rahi he
 This unity will form the basis of change in 2019
 ’gyatavya he ki shivasena pehle hi yah spasht kar chuki he ki vah 2019 kaa chunaav bhaajapa ke saath nahin ladegi
 The TDP, the other major constituent of the ruling NDA at the Center, also expressed disappointment over the general budget presented recently
 kendriya vitt mantri arun jetali dwaara sansad main pesh aam bajet main madhyam varg ko niraashaa haath lagane ke aaropon ke bare main puche jane par surajevaala ne kaha ki modi sarkaar ne madhyam varg or naukareepesha logon ko keval jumalon se chalaa he, diya kuch nahin
 The biggest hit of demonetisation and GST also occurred on this category
 unhone kaha ki vitt mantri ke mutabik sabase zyada tex bhi yahi varg detaa he
 They feel that it is this class which is the most wealthy while the truth is that it is the class that is the most hard working and honest
 is varg ko aaj mahangaai kii badi keemat chukaani pad rahi he
 That is why the middle class has understood this very well that in the Modi government 'things are not much and nothing is done
 ’ While presenting the General Budget for the year 2018-19, the Finance Minister has not given any major relief in the matter of income tax despite praising the working class for paying taxes
 is saal karnataka sahit aath rajyon main hone ja rahe vidhansabha chunaavon main congress kii ranneeti puche jane par surajevaala ne kaha, ‘tarakkee ke lihaaj se sabase mahatvapurn rajya karnataka main congress phir se satta main aegi, aisa hamaara vishwaas he
 The way we have introduced a model of development in Karnataka, be it the ewe bill or other schemes of the Government of Karnataka, now the Government of India also believes that they should be implemented across the country
 ’ He said that the trailer for the elections in the next phase in Madhya Pradesh, Chhattisgarh, Rajasthan etc
, came two days ago in the by-election in Rajasthan where the Congress won two Lok Sabha and one Assembly seats
 unhone kaha, ‘yah gussa akele vasundhara raaje sarkaar ke khilaaf nahin he
 This is the wind of the people being cheated by the Modi government and the jungle of the Raje government
 ’ pichley saptaah ghoshit hue up-chunaavon ke nateezon main congress ne ajmer or alvar loksabhaa tathaa mandalgarh vidhansabha seat jeet kar sattarudh bhaajapa ko jhatka diya kyonki yah teenon siten bhagava dal ke paas thim
 Assembly elections are due in Karnataka, Meghalaya, Tripura, Nagaland, Madhya Pradesh, Chhattisgarh, Rajasthan and Mizoram in the year 2018
 party adhyaksh ke taur par rahul gandhi kii teen praathamiktaayen puche jane par surajevaala ne kaha ki unki pehali praathamikta he akhil bhartiya congress or desh bhar main isaki ikaayiyon ke sanghathan kaa punargathan or badlaav
 His other priority is to formulate and implement a 'vision' so that farmers can get proper benefits of their produce
 is vijan main nijee evam sarkari kshetron main naukariyon ke srijan ke upaay honge
 He said, 'modiji's model will help 12 industrialists, while in Rahul Gandhi's model, medium and small scale industries sector will have to be given priority, market and loans for them
 ’ unhone kaha ki teesri praathamikta he saamaajik shanti evam bhaichaare kii bahaali
 'modiji has forgotten that when the social fabric breaks, the wheel of development stops
 ’ rahul ke congress adhyaksh banane ke baad party kaa pehla mahadhiveshan kab hoga, yah puche jane par unhone kaha ki abhi isaki taarikh nishchit nahin hui he
 But in the year 2019 and beyond, the Congress will give a new vision to the structure of this country through this session
 tippaniyan VIDEO: Rahul Gandhi, Congress express objection in sixth row during Republic Day parade gujarat chunaav ke baad congress par ‘soft hindutv’ kii raah par chalane kii dharna ke kaaran alpsankhyak virgon ke man main congress kii dharmanirpekshata ke ruukh ko lekar ashanka hone ke bare main poochne par unhone kaha, ‘dharm vyaktigat aasthaa kaa vishay he

 You must have heard and seen many sun temples, but the ancient sun temple located at Dev in Aurangabad district of Bihar is unique
 kaha jaataa he ki is mandir kaa nirmaan swayan bhagwaan vishwakarma ne ek raat main kii thi
 It is the only Sun Temple in the country whose door faces west
 aisa kaha jaataa he kichhath puja ke dauraanis mandir ke darshan or yahaan surya pujan se har manokamana puri hoti he
 There is no clear evidence of the construction of this temple, but it is said that this temple was built one and a half million years ago
 chhath parv ke maukey par yahaan lakhon log bhagwaan bhaskar kii aradhana ke liye jutate hai
 The historic Tretayugin western-facing Sun Temple is noted for its unique artistic grandeur as well as its history
 aurangabad se 18 kilometre dur dev sthit surya mandir kareeb sau feet ooncha he
 It is believed that this temple was built by Lord Vishwakarma himself in Treta Yuga
 dedh lakh varsh purana yah surya mandir kaale or bhure pattharon kii nayab shilpkaaree se bana yah surya mandir oreisha ke puri sthit jagannatha mandir se miltaa-julata he
